// Create a module that implements an AND gate.

// Hint: Verilog has separate bitwise-AND (&) and logical-AND (&&) operators, like C. 
// Since we're working with a one-bit here, it doesn't matter which we choose.

module top_module( 
    input a, 
    input b, 
    output out );
    wire and_out;
    assign and_out = a && b;
    assign out = and_out;
endmodule
